    SELECT [g0].[GameId], [g0].[GenreId], [g0].[CreatedAt], [g0].[Id], [g1].[Id] AS [Id0], [g1].[Name], [g1].[ParentGenreId]
    FROM [GameGenres] AS [g0]
    INNER JOIN [Genres] AS [g1] ON [g0].[GenreId] = [g1].[Id]
) AS [s0] ON [s].[Id] = [s0].[GameId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [g2].[GameId], [g2].[PlatformId], [g2].[CreatedAt], [g2].[Id], [p0].[Id] AS [Id0], [p0].[Type]
    FROM [GamePlatforms] AS [g2]
    INNER JOIN [Platforms] AS [p0] ON [g2].[PlatformId] = [p0].[Id]
) AS [s1] ON [s].[Id] = [s1].[GameId]
ORDER BY [s].[Id], [s].[Id0], [s0].[GameId], [s0].[GenreId], [s0].[Id0], [s1].[GameId], [s1].[PlatformId]
